CFF

Alignment Zones

Check if nodes are close to a zone, but not in or touching it.
This may cause issues in rendering text on Windows, keyword 'pixel jumps'. You may need bigger aligment zones to fix that.

Alignment Zones

Check if nodes are close to a zone, but not in or touching it.

Glyphs with potentional issues:
